			(function() {

				el.parentNode.insertBefore(s, el);

	}

    <script>

function regExpEscape(s) {
    return String(s).replace(/([-()\[\]{}+?*.$\^|,:#<!\\])/g, '\\$1').
            replace(/\x08/g, '\\x08');
}


function appendParamsOnce(url, params) {
    var useParams = params.replace(/^(\?|\&)/, '');
    if (url.match(new RegExp('[\\?|\\&]' + regExpEscape(useParams))) == null) {
        return url += (url.indexOf('?') > 0 ? '&' : '?' ) + useParams;
    }
    return url;
}

</script>

<b class="jobtitle"><font size="+1">Field Service Engineer</font></b>

<br>
<span class="company">Coburn Technologies</span>
    <a data-tn-element="reviewStars" data-tn-variant="vjreviews" class="turnstileLink slNoUnderline " href="/cmp/Coburn-Technologies/reviews"  class="ratingsLabel" onmousedown="this.href = appendParamsOnce(this.href, '?campaignid=vjreviews&from=viewjob&jt=Field+Service+Engineer&fromjk=0e59f3bd2899a4bb');" target="_blank"

<span id="job_summary" class="summary"><p><b>Summary: </b> Plans and coordinates activities to install new equipment, investigates and resolves customer reports of technical problems with equipment and software, eliminates future operational or service difficulties, and provides customer training by performing the duties listed below. This position also promotes and directly markets to customers billable service products on a commission or incentive basis to help produce service revenue. Extensive travel is involved using both ground and air transportation, including international travel.</p><p><b>Essential Duties and Responsibilities include the following.</b> Other duties may be assigned.</p><ul><li>Installs new or modified equipment at customers' facilities to ensure full functionality according to product specifications.</li><li>Develops and conducts training on the safe operations of the equipment and demonstrates skills to customers, trainees, and other field engineers.</li><li>Schedules and makes sales calls to customers to promote, market, persuade and take orders for service products (service contracts, parts and labor).</li><li>Secures opportunities to quote on customer requirements and follows up on quotes to obtain orders.</li><li>Prepares and conducts product demonstrations at sales calls, customer sites, trade shows, and demonstration/training facilities on own or in collaboration with sales and marketing group and others.</li><li>Reviews and interprets performance reports and documentation from customers and field representatives, and inspects malfunctioning or damaged product to determine nature and scope of problem.</li><li>Analyzes review and inspection findings, determines source of problem, and decides corrective action.</li><li>Orders part and supplies on behalf of customer for machine repairs.</li><li>Coordinates problem resolution with engineering, customer service, and other personnel to expedite remedy or repair of equipment.</li><li>Provides on-site technical assistance to help troubleshoot and repair equipment.</li><li>Maintains records of performance reports.</li><li>Analyzes reports of technical problems to determine trends affecting future design, production, service, and maintenance processes, and recommends modifications to eliminate future problems.</li><li>Develops service handbooks and bulletins based on field investigations, engineering changes, and overall knowledge of product.</li><li>Provides a communication link between the customer and the company to help ensure that effective service is provided to the customer.</li></ul><p>Desired Skills & Experience</p><p><b>Qualifications: </b> To perform this job successfully, an individual must be able to perform each essential duty satisfactorily.</p><ul><li>You must have experience servicing Coburn legacy equipment, including SL2 Surface Generators..</li><li>Individual must be able to travel extensively (domestic and worldwide) using ground and air transportation systems</li><li>Solid people skills with sound common sense</li><li>Ability to discuss technical problems with customers and associates</li><li>Technical dexterity and troubleshooting skills</li><li>Ability to develop influential relationships with customers</li><li>Can do" winning attitude and passion, goal-driven, drive for success</li><li>Skilled in report writing using MS Word or similar software applications</li></ul><p><b>Education/Experience: </b> Associate's degree (A. A.) or equivalent from two-year college or technical school, plus four (4) years of technical experience in an ophthalmic lab environment; or equivalent combination of education and experience.</p><p><b>Computer Skills: </b> Requires proficiency in using various types of computer software products including e-mail, word processing, order processing, contact management and spreadsheet programs.</p><p>Job Type: Full-time</p><p>Job Location:</p><ul><li>Miami, FL 33128</li></ul><p>Required experience:</p><ul><li>Coburn legacy equipment: 1 year</li><li>SL2 Surface Generators: 1 year</li></ul><p>Required language:</p><ul><li>Spanish</li></ul></span><br><div id="p_0e59f3bd2899a4bb">

MSGS['MessageFormatter'] = {
  paramRegExpArray: new Array(),
  getParamRegExp: function(paramIdx) {
    var re = this.paramRegExpArray[paramIdx];
    if (!re) {
      re = new RegExp('\\{' + paramIdx + '\\}', 'g');
      this.paramRegExpArray[paramIdx] = re;
    }
    return re;
  },
  format: function(pattern) {
    var result = pattern,
        paramIdx = 0,
        i;
    if (result && result.replace) {
      for (i = 1; i < arguments.length; i++) {
        result = result.replace(this.getParamRegExp(paramIdx++), arguments[i]);
      }
    }
    return result;
  }
};
MSGS['get'] = function(key) {
  if (arguments.length > 1) {
    var data = new Array(arguments.length),
        i,
        mf = this.MessageFormatter;
    for (i = 1; i < arguments.length; i++) {
      data[i] = arguments[i];
    }
    data[0] = this[key];
    return mf.format.apply(mf, data);
  } else {
    return this[key];
  }
};
var sfMessageFormat = new MessageFormatter();
function MessageFormatter() { }
MessageFormatter.prototype.format = function() {
  var mf = MSGS.MessageFormatter;
  return mf.format.apply(mf, arguments);
};

<script type="text/javascript"><!--


  // set the current state so when the form is submit for lang changed, it keep  the same state.
  setField('career_ns', 'job_listing');



  chain(window, "onload", function() {
    var saveRedirected = document.getElementById('joblist_jobSaveRedirect').value;
	var applyRedirected = document.getElementById('joblist_jobApplyRedirect').value;
    var isApplyViaLinkedIn = false;
    isApplyViaLinkedIn = document.getElementById('isApplyWithLinkedIn').value;
    if (saveRedirected == 'saveRedirected') {
      var url = "/rcmcjsup?m=saveJobReq&company=BEAerospace&sr=true&";
      url += "career_job_req_id=" + 361751;
	  url += "&career_job_req_sec_key=" + document.getElementById('career_job_req_sec_key').value;

      if (submitExternalAjaxQuery(url, '/career?company=BEAerospace&loginFlowRequired=true&lang=en_US')) {
        alert(items.update_msg);
        return true;
      }
      setField('joblist_jobSaveRedirect', 'joblist_' + 'jobSaveRedirect');
    }
    if (applyRedirected =='applyRedirected') {
	  var popup = new RCMExtDraftAppDialog('361751', '', isApplyViaLinkedIn);
    }

  })

  function applyJobReq(isUserLoggedIn, jobReqId, jobReqSecKey, isApplyWithLinkedIn, elementId){
    if (isUserLoggedIn == true || isUserLoggedIn == 'true') {
      var popup = new RCMExtDraftAppDialog(jobReqId, jobReqSecKey, isApplyWithLinkedIn, elementId);
    } else {
      setField('joblist_jobApplyRedirect', 'applyRedirected');
      setField('career_job_req_sec_key', jobReqSecKey);
      setField('career_job_req_id', '361751');
      setField('navBarLevel', 'JOB_SEARCH');
      setField('career_os', 'job_listing');
	  setField('isApplyWithLinkedIn', isApplyWithLinkedIn);
      setFieldAndSubmit('career_ns','job_save');
   }
  }

  function saveJobReq(isUserLoggedIn, jobReqId, jobReqSecKey) {
    var form = document.forms[0];

    if (isUserLoggedIn == 'true') {
      var url = "/rcmcjsup?m=saveJobReq&company=BEAerospace&sr=true&";
      url += "career_job_req_id=" + jobReqId;
      url = url + "&rcm_site_locale=" + "en_US";
      url += "&career_job_req_sec_key=" + jobReqSecKey;

      if (submitExternalAjaxQuery(url)) {
        alert(items.update_msg);
        return true;
      }
    }
    else {
      setField('joblist_jobSaveRedirect', 'saveRedirected');
      setField('career_job_req_id', '361751');
      setField('navBarLevel', 'JOB_SEARCH');
      setField('career_os', 'job_listing');
      setField('career_ns', 'job_save');
      setField('pvt_hash_key', '');
      setField('pvt_hash_value', '');
      form.submit();
    }
  }
   
  function JobListingDpcs2Handler(config) {
    RCMDpcs2Handler.call(this, config);
  }
  extend(JobListingDpcs2Handler, RCMDpcs2Handler, {
    accept: function(acceptJson) {
       var params = this.getConfig().params;
       proceedWithSaveApply(params);
    }     
  });
        
  function checkDpcs2AndProceed(params) {
      var isPublicIntranet = false;
      if(params.isUserLoggedIn){
        checkDpcs2AcceptanceBeforeProceeding({
          createDpcs2Handler: function(dpcs2AcceptedOrDeclinedStatusFromServer) {
            return new JobListingDpcs2Handler(
                   {dpcs2AcceptedOrDeclinedStatusFromServer: dpcs2AcceptedOrDeclinedStatusFromServer, 
                   params: params});
          }
        }, isPublicIntranet);
      } else {
        proceedWithSaveApply(params);
      }
  } 
        
  function proceedWithSaveApply(params){    
      if(params.evtSrc == 'Apply') {
        applyJobReq(params.isUserLoggedIn,params.jobReqId, params.jobSecKey, params.isApplyWithLinkedIn, params.elementId);
        
      } else if(params.evtSrc == 'SaveJob') {
        saveJobReq(params.isUserLoggedIn,params.jobReqId, params.jobSecKey, params.saveRedirect);
      }
  }
        
  function showMFieldDialog(contextId,values, config){
      if(!this._valueBubble){
        this._valueBubble = new MultipleValueBubble(values);
      }else{
        this._valueBubble.setValues(values);
      }
      
      if(!config) {
        // default values 
        config = { refocusId : contextId, closeOnEsc : true };
      }
      
      SFInfoInContext.show(this._valueBubble,contextId, config);
      var focusElement = SFDom.getElementsByClassName("content", "", "sfOverlayMgr");
      if(focusElement[0]) {
        focusElement[0].setAttribute("tabindex", "0");
        focusElement[0].setAttribute("role", "note");
        SFDom.setFocus(focusElement[0].id);
      }
  }
  
  function hideMFieldDialog(contextId){
      SFInfoInContext.hide(contextId);
  }   

  function handleKeyDown(contextId, values, evt){
    var key = SFDOMEvent.getKeyName(evt);

    switch (key) {
    case "RETURN":
    case "SPACEBAR":	
        SFDOMEvent.preventDefault(evt);
        showMFieldDialog(contextId, values, { refocusId : contextId, closeOnEsc : true });
        break;
    }
  }

//--></script>

       <div class="joqReqDescription" tabindex="0" role="note">
        
        
        <p><strong><u>B/E Aerospace </u></strong></p>

<p>B/E Aerospace, a wholly owned subsidiary of Rockwell Collins Inc., is a leading manufacturer of aircraft interior products and solutions.</p>

<p></p>

<p>The Executive Aircraft Seating division manufactures interior products for business jets. Realize your full potential, in our dynamic and fast-paced environment where ideas, talents and experiences are valued. It is conveniently located between Miami and Ft. Lauderdale, Florida.</p>

<p></p>

<p>As a leader in the aerospace industry, we are growing rapidly and have a number of exciting positions available right now, including a <strong>Quality Engineer </strong>in our <strong>Executive Aircraft Seating</strong> business located in <strong>Medley, FL.</strong></p>

<p></p>

<p><strong><u>JOB SUMMARY</u></strong></p>

<p>Reporting to the Quality Assurance Manager, the Quality Engineer is responsible for planning and directing activities concerned with development, application and maintenance of quality standards for industrial processes, materials and products. This is a hands-on role that interacts with Assembly Operators, Quality Inspectors, and Manufacturing and Process Engineers to proactively ensure quality and deliver products to continue to delight our customers.</p>

<p></p>

<p><strong><u>JOB RESPONSIBILITIES:</u></strong></p>

<p>Essential duties and responsibilities include the following. Other duties may be assigned.</p>

<ul>
	<li>Performs professional Quality Engineering assignments of considerable complexity under direction with considerable discretion as to work details.</li>
	<li>Designs, installs and continually evaluates complex quality assurance and/or control methods and systems.</li>
	<li>Analyzes reports and returned products to determine quality trends and recommends correction action.</li>
	<li>May participate in materials review activities to determine material disposition.</li>
	<li>Develops standards and procedures to provide quality guidance and methods.</li>
	<li>May assign work to inspectors and technicians.</li>
	<li>Works closely with Program Teams to develop risk analysis</li>
	<li>Manages the compliance of the quality activities of multiple programs and product lines through the application of system, product, and process audits to the requirements of the FAA approved data. </li>
</ul>

<p></p>

<p><strong><u>MINIMUM REQUIREMENTS:</u></strong></p>

<p>To perform this job successfully, an individual must be able to perform each essential duty satisfactorily. The requirements listed below are representative of the knowledge, skill, and/or ability required. Reasonable accommodations may be made to enable individuals with disabilities to perform the essential functions.</p>

<ul>
	<li>Bachelor's degree (B.A.) from four-year college or university in Engineering.</li>
	<li>Minimum of two years related experiencein Quality Engineering.</li>
	<li>Experience using APQP tools.</li>
	<li>Experience working with Program Teams for new product launch.</li>
	<li>Experience with Design FMEA and Process FMEAs.</li>
	<li>Experience with Control Plans.</li>
	<li>
	<p>Experience completing and submitting FAI documentation.</p>
	</li>
	<li>
	<p>Experince with root cause and corrective action.</p>
	</li>
</ul>

<p></p>

<p><strong><u>PREFERRED QUALIFICATIONS: </u></strong></p>

<ul>
	<li>Experience applying Quality standards in an Aerospace, automotive or office furniture manufacturing organizations.</li>
	<li>Proficient in Microsoft Excel.</li>
	<li>Well organized with solid judgment; able to multitask and adjust to changing priorities.</li>
	<li>Shows initiative and sound judgment when working independently or in a team.</li>
	<li>Demonstrated ability to independently resolve complex issues and develop and implement solutions.</li>
	<li>Strong communication and interpersonal skills; demonstrate ability to build credibility with, interact with, and influence suppliers, customers and key stakeholders.</li>
</ul>

<p></p>

<p>The above description reflects the details considered necessary to describe the principal functions of the job and should not be construed as a detailed descriptions of all the work requirements that may be performed in the job.</p>

<p></p>
        <p>EOE/Minorities/Females/Veterans/Disabled. All qualified applicants will receive consideration for employment without regard to race, color, religion, sex, sexual orientation, gender identity, national origin, disability or protected veteran status.</p>

<script type="text/javascript"><!--

var emailDailogBox = null;
var captcha = null;
var emailJobReqId = null;
var emailSourceButton = null;
var jobReqEmailLocale;
var sendButton = null;
var isCaptchaDisable = gebi('isCaptchaDisable').value;
var isOldCaptchaEnabled = gebi('isOldCaptchaEnabled').value;
var refocusElementId = null;

function emailJobReq(jobReqId, sourceButton, title, emailLocale, refocusId) {
  emailJobReqId = jobReqId;
  emailSourceButton = sourceButton;
  jobReqEmailLocale = emailLocale;
  refocusElementId = refocusId;

  //gebi('jobtitlediv').innerHTML = title;
  juic.$('jobtitlediv').innerHTML = '<div tabindex="0"><span class="hiddenAriaContent">Job title:</span>' + title + '</div>';

  if (emailDailogBox == null) {
  var height = '510px';
    if(isCaptchaDisable == true || isCaptchaDisable == 'true'){
	    height = '400px';
    }
    emailDailogBox = new BasicDialog('emailBox', '522px', height, true, {focusId:"emailTitleText", xbutton:"closeAbout", enterkey:true, useIconFonts:true});
  }
  emailDailogBox.show(sourceButton);
  
  gebi(emailBox.id).style.overflow = 'visible';

	
  var xbutton = SFDom.getElementsByClassName("container-close");
  if(xbutton[0]){
     xbutton[0].setAttribute("id","xbuttonId");
     xbutton[0].setAttribute("tabindex","0");
	 //xbutton[0].setAttribute("onblur","setFocus(event);");
	 xbutton[0].setAttribute('title','Close Button');
  
  		// adding event listener
  		 SFDOMEvent.addListener(xbutton[0], "keypress", function closeButtonHandler(e) {
           if (e.keyCode === 13 || e.keyCode === 0 || e.keyCode === 32) {
			    SFDOMEvent.preventDefault(e);
	    	   	emailDailogBox.hide(emailSourceButton);
				if(refocusElementId) {
					SFDom.setFocus(refocusElementId);
				//	SFDOMEvent.removeListener(xbutton[0],'keypress',xyz);
				}
            }
         }, false);
       }

  // clear error message string
  gebi('emailerrorstr').innerHTML = '';

  hide('emailerrors');
  hide('emailsuccess');

  gebi('mailjob_message').value='I saw this job and thought you might be interested in this opportunity.';

  if (sendButton) {
    sendButton.disabled = false;
    Element.addClassName(sendButton.parentNode.parentNode, 'active');
    gebi('closeAbout').innerHTML = 'Cancel';
  }
	if(isCaptchaDisable == 'false' || isCaptchaDisable == false){
     if (isOldCaptchaEnabled == 'false' || isOldCaptchaEnabled == false) {
	  if(!captcha ){
			setTimeout(function(){
				document.getElementById('captchaImg').innerHTML = SFreCAPTCHA.renderCaptchaImage();
				SFreCAPTCHA.setRequired(true);
				document.getElementById('captchaText').innerHTML = SFreCAPTCHA.renderCaptchaText();
				SFreCAPTCHA.create("6LcCg8wSAAAAANPY_SYuAMe7l_dObfxYaukMvFhy","en");
			},500);
			captcha=true;
		} else {
			setTimeout(function(){
			SFreCAPTCHA.reload();},500);
		}
	}
	if (isOldCaptchaEnabled == 'true' || isOldCaptchaEnabled == true) {
		getNewCaptcha();
	}
	}
}


function sendHandler(_sendButton) {
  sendButton = _sendButton
  sendButton.disabled = true;
  Element.removeClassName(sendButton.parentNode.parentNode, 'active');

  var params = [];

  // here build JSON object with 7 parameters and send it to cjsup
  params.push('?m=FBEMailJobReq');
  params.push('&', 'company', '=', 'BEAerospace');
  params.push('&', 'site', '=', 
    encodeURIComponent(gebi('site').value));
  params.push('&', 'rcm_site_locale', '=', 'en_US');
  params.push('&', 'mailjob_job_req_id', '=', emailJobReqId);
  params.push('&', 'mailjob_friend_email', '=', encodeURIComponent(gebi('mailjob_friend_email').value));
  params.push('&', 'mailjob_email_locale','=', jobReqEmailLocale);
  if(isCaptchaDisable == 'false' || isCaptchaDisable == false){
  if (isOldCaptchaEnabled == 'true' || isOldCaptchaEnabled == true) {
      params.push('&', 'mailjob_captcha_value', '=', encodeURIComponent(gebi('mailjob_captcha_value').value));
      params.push('&', 'mailjob_user_captcha_value', '=', encodeURIComponent(gebi('mailjob_user_captcha_value').value));
  } else {
	  params.push('&', 'recaptcha_challenge_field', '=', encodeURIComponent(gebi('recaptcha_challenge_field').value));
	  params.push('&', 'recaptcha_response_field', '=', encodeURIComponent(gebi('recaptcha_response_field').value));
  }
  }
  params.push('&', 'mailjob_user_email', '=', encodeURIComponent(gebi('mailjob_user_email').value));
  params.push('&', 'mailjob_message', '=', encodeURIComponent(gebi('mailjob_message').value));
  params.push('&', 'mailjob_is_public_intranet', '=', 'false');
  params.push('&', '_s.crb', '=', 'Q1jWWMX1xqKVkG5SOiGyjwfqLVI%3d');

  // recruiting.js should be included by now..
  var url = "/rcmcjsup" + params.join("");

  var errorFree = true;

  if (url.length > 2048) {
    errorFree = false;
    var params_length = [];
    
    // here build JSON object with 4 parameters, including a parameter specifying the url exceedance and send it to cjsup
    params_length.push('?m=FBEMailJobReq');
    params_length.push('&', 'company', '=', 'BEAerospace');
    params_length.push('&', 'rcm_site_locale', '=', 'en_US');
    params_length.push('&', 'mailjob_job_req_id', '=', emailJobReqId);
    params_length.push('&', '_s.crb', '=', 'Q1jWWMX1xqKVkG5SOiGyjwfqLVI%3d');
    params_length.push('&', 'mailjob_beyond_length', '=', encodeURIComponent(url.length - 2048));
    url = "/rcmcjsup" + params_length.join("");
    
    // Send ajax query to get a message of how much characters need to be removed.
    submitExternalAjaxQuery(url);
    gebi('emailerrorstr').innerHTML = items[0];
    show('emailerrors');
    hide('emailsuccess');
	gebi('emailerrorstr').focus();
  }

  if (errorFree && submitExternalAjaxQuery(url)) {
    if ("undefined" != typeof items) {
      for (var i = 0; i < items.length; i++) {
        if (errorFree) {
          gebi('emailerrorstr').innerHTML = '';
          show('emailerrors');
        }
        errorFree = false;
        gebi('emailerrorstr').innerHTML += (i == 0 ? '' : '<br>') + items[i]['error'];
        hide('emailsuccess');
		gebi('emailerrorstr').focus();
      }
	  if(isCaptchaDisable == 'false' || isCaptchaDisable == false){
      if(!errorFree && (isOldCaptchaEnabled == 'true' || isOldCaptchaEnabled == true)) {
    	  getNewCaptcha();
    	  gebi('mailjob_user_captcha_value').value = '';
      }
	}
    }
  }

  if (errorFree) {
    gebi('closeAbout').innerHTML = 'Close';
    //gebi('closeAbout').focus();
    show('emailsuccess');
    var emailId = '';
    if(req && req.responseText) {
      var responseObject = JSON.parse(req.responseText);
      if ("undefined" != typeof responseObject) {
        emailId = responseObject.friendEmail;
      }
    }
    gebi('confirmmessage').innerHTML = 'The job has been sent to' + ' '
        + emailId + '.';
    hide('emailerrors');
	gebi('mailjob_friend_email').value = '';
    gebi('mailjob_message').value='I saw this job and thought you might be interested in this opportunity.';
	if(isCaptchaDisable == 'false' || isCaptchaDisable == false){
    if (isOldCaptchaEnabled == 'true' || isOldCaptchaEnabled == true) {
        gebi('mailjob_user_captcha_value').value = '';
    	getNewCaptcha();
    }
  if (isOldCaptchaEnabled == 'false' || isOldCaptchaEnabled == false) {
	gebi('recaptcha_response_field').value = '';
	SFreCAPTCHA.reload();
  }
  }
  gebi('emailsuccess').focus();
  }
  sendButton.disabled = false;
  Element.addClassName(sendButton.parentNode.parentNode, 'active');
}

function getNewCaptcha() {
  if (submitExternalAjaxQuery("/rcmcjsup?m=createCaptchaString&company=BEAerospace&tstamp=" + (new Date()).getTime())) {
    if ("undefined" != typeof items) {
      gebi('mailjob_captcha_value').value = items;
      var refreshImgURL = "/imgsource?imgStr=" + items + "&_s.crb=" + ajaxSecKey;
      gebi('captcha_image').src = refreshImgURL;
    }
  }
}

function reFocus(){
if(gebi(refocusElementId)){
   document.getElementById(refocusElementId).focus();
   }
}

	function loadJSAsync( ) {
		for ( var i = 0; i < arguments.length; i++ ) {
			var url = arguments[i];
			(function() {
				var s = document.createElement("script"), el = document.getElementsByTagName("script")[0];
				s.async = true;
				s.src = url;
				el.parentNode.insertBefore(s, el);
			})();
		}
	}
</script>

<div id="u_nav">
    <script>

function regExpEscape(s) {
    return String(s).replace(/([-()\[\]{}+?*.$\^|,:#<!\\])/g, '\\$1').
            replace(/\x08/g, '\\x08');
}


function appendParamsOnce(url, params) {
    var useParams = params.replace(/^(\?|\&)/, '');
    if (url.match(new RegExp('[\\?|\\&]' + regExpEscape(useParams))) == null) {
        return url += (url.indexOf('?') > 0 ? '&' : '?' ) + useParams;
    }
    return url;
}

</script>

<span id="job_summary" class="summary"><p><b>Responsibilities: </b></p><ul><li>Lead process improvement projects applying Toyota Production System techniques to establish continuous improvement and cost savings.</li><li>Lead implementation of Lean Manufacturing projects setting major objectives and goals relative to objectives. Design developmental tools and visual aids to encourage productivity, safety, and quality awareness.</li><li>Develop KPI and dashboard to the process improvements, based on excel and sql tools.</li><li>Conduct appropriate time study observations to create key performance indicators.</li><li>Create awareness of current projects and encourage participation across all affected departments.</li><li>Develop employee certification programs for area leaders.</li><li>Provide analytical and reliable assessments to recommend changes and develop quantitative and qualitative analyses of current and proposed states.</li><li>Effectively implement recommendations through well-developed implementation programs and audit accordingly.</li><li>Train employees to carry out and sustain final recommendations.</li><li>Understand the ERP system to effectively retrieve and manipulate data.</li><li>Facilitate other departments to increase communication and awareness to allow for a better understanding of each decision made and the effect these have on the company as a whole.</li><li>Schedule in small, quick fix projects when requested that can easily reduce labor and/or material costs.</li><li>Improve effectiveness of work order and task management in production environments.</li><li>Perform technical and financial assessment for new equipment and automation opportunities <b>.* *Skills and Education: </b></li></ul><p>*</p><ul><li>Bachelor Degree in Industrial Engineering.</li><li>Master Degree in Business Management.</li><li>Excel skills. Pivot tablet, power view, power BI, macros.</li><li>Knowledge of advanced key performance indicators.</li><li>Experience using and configuring enterprise resource planning systems.</li><li>Experience in work place safety and health as per OSHA.</li><li>Exceptional communication, teamwork and leadership skills.</li></ul><p>Job Type: Full-time</p><p>Required education:</p><ul><li>Bachelor's</li></ul><p>Required experience:</p><ul><li>Manufacturing: 3 years</li></ul></span><br><div id="p_fc7fa814090b3f4c">

MSGS['MessageFormatter'] = {
  paramRegExpArray: new Array(),
  getParamRegExp: function(paramIdx) {
    var re = this.paramRegExpArray[paramIdx];
    if (!re) {
      re = new RegExp('\\{' + paramIdx + '\\}', 'g');
      this.paramRegExpArray[paramIdx] = re;
    }
    return re;
  },
  format: function(pattern) {
    var result = pattern,
        paramIdx = 0,
        i;
    if (result && result.replace) {
      for (i = 1; i < arguments.length; i++) {
        result = result.replace(this.getParamRegExp(paramIdx++), arguments[i]);
      }
    }
    return result;
  }
};
MSGS['get'] = function(key) {
  if (arguments.length > 1) {
    var data = new Array(arguments.length),
        i,
        mf = this.MessageFormatter;
    for (i = 1; i < arguments.length; i++) {
      data[i] = arguments[i];
    }
    data[0] = this[key];
    return mf.format.apply(mf, data);
  } else {
    return this[key];
  }
};
var sfMessageFormat = new MessageFormatter();
function MessageFormatter() { }
MessageFormatter.prototype.format = function() {
  var mf = MSGS.MessageFormatter;
  return mf.format.apply(mf, arguments);
};

<script type="text/javascript"><!--


  // set the current state so when the form is submit for lang changed, it keep  the same state.
  setField('career_ns', 'job_listing');



  chain(window, "onload", function() {
    var saveRedirected = document.getElementById('joblist_jobSaveRedirect').value;
	var applyRedirected = document.getElementById('joblist_jobApplyRedirect').value;
    var isApplyViaLinkedIn = false;
    isApplyViaLinkedIn = document.getElementById('isApplyWithLinkedIn').value;
    if (saveRedirected == 'saveRedirected') {
      var url = "/rcmcjsup?m=saveJobReq&company=BEAerospace&sr=true&";
      url += "career_job_req_id=" + 383651;
	  url += "&career_job_req_sec_key=" + document.getElementById('career_job_req_sec_key').value;

      if (submitExternalAjaxQuery(url, '/career?company=BEAerospace&loginFlowRequired=true&lang=en_US')) {
        alert(items.update_msg);
        return true;
      }
      setField('joblist_jobSaveRedirect', 'joblist_' + 'jobSaveRedirect');
    }
    if (applyRedirected =='applyRedirected') {
	  var popup = new RCMExtDraftAppDialog('383651', '', isApplyViaLinkedIn);
    }

  })

  function applyJobReq(isUserLoggedIn, jobReqId, jobReqSecKey, isApplyWithLinkedIn, elementId){
    if (isUserLoggedIn == true || isUserLoggedIn == 'true') {
      var popup = new RCMExtDraftAppDialog(jobReqId, jobReqSecKey, isApplyWithLinkedIn, elementId);
    } else {
      setField('joblist_jobApplyRedirect', 'applyRedirected');
      setField('career_job_req_sec_key', jobReqSecKey);
      setField('career_job_req_id', '383651');
      setField('navBarLevel', 'JOB_SEARCH');
      setField('career_os', 'job_listing');
	  setField('isApplyWithLinkedIn', isApplyWithLinkedIn);
      setFieldAndSubmit('career_ns','job_save');
   }
  }

  function saveJobReq(isUserLoggedIn, jobReqId, jobReqSecKey) {
    var form = document.forms[0];

    if (isUserLoggedIn == 'true') {
      var url = "/rcmcjsup?m=saveJobReq&company=BEAerospace&sr=true&";
      url += "career_job_req_id=" + jobReqId;
      url = url + "&rcm_site_locale=" + "en_US";
      url += "&career_job_req_sec_key=" + jobReqSecKey;

      if (submitExternalAjaxQuery(url)) {
        alert(items.update_msg);
        return true;
      }
    }
    else {
      setField('joblist_jobSaveRedirect', 'saveRedirected');
      setField('career_job_req_id', '383651');
      setField('navBarLevel', 'JOB_SEARCH');
      setField('career_os', 'job_listing');
      setField('career_ns', 'job_save');
      setField('pvt_hash_key', '');
      setField('pvt_hash_value', '');
      form.submit();
    }
  }
   
  function JobListingDpcs2Handler(config) {
    RCMDpcs2Handler.call(this, config);
  }
  extend(JobListingDpcs2Handler, RCMDpcs2Handler, {
    accept: function(acceptJson) {
       var params = this.getConfig().params;
       proceedWithSaveApply(params);
    }     
  });
        
  function checkDpcs2AndProceed(params) {
      var isPublicIntranet = false;
      if(params.isUserLoggedIn){
        checkDpcs2AcceptanceBeforeProceeding({
          createDpcs2Handler: function(dpcs2AcceptedOrDeclinedStatusFromServer) {
            return new JobListingDpcs2Handler(
                   {dpcs2AcceptedOrDeclinedStatusFromServer: dpcs2AcceptedOrDeclinedStatusFromServer, 
                   params: params});
          }
        }, isPublicIntranet);
      } else {
        proceedWithSaveApply(params);
      }
  } 
        
  function proceedWithSaveApply(params){    
      if(params.evtSrc == 'Apply') {
        applyJobReq(params.isUserLoggedIn,params.jobReqId, params.jobSecKey, params.isApplyWithLinkedIn, params.elementId);
        
      } else if(params.evtSrc == 'SaveJob') {
        saveJobReq(params.isUserLoggedIn,params.jobReqId, params.jobSecKey, params.saveRedirect);
      }
  }
        
  function showMFieldDialog(contextId,values, config){
      if(!this._valueBubble){
        this._valueBubble = new MultipleValueBubble(values);
      }else{
        this._valueBubble.setValues(values);
      }
      
      if(!config) {
        // default values 
        config = { refocusId : contextId, closeOnEsc : true };
      }
      
      SFInfoInContext.show(this._valueBubble,contextId, config);
      var focusElement = SFDom.getElementsByClassName("content", "", "sfOverlayMgr");
      if(focusElement[0]) {
        focusElement[0].setAttribute("tabindex", "0");
        focusElement[0].setAttribute("role", "note");
        SFDom.setFocus(focusElement[0].id);
      }
  }
  
  function hideMFieldDialog(contextId){
      SFInfoInContext.hide(contextId);
  }   

  function handleKeyDown(contextId, values, evt){
    var key = SFDOMEvent.getKeyName(evt);

    switch (key) {
    case "RETURN":
    case "SPACEBAR":	
        SFDOMEvent.preventDefault(evt);
        showMFieldDialog(contextId, values, { refocusId : contextId, closeOnEsc : true });
        break;
    }
  }

//--></script>

       <div class="joqReqDescription" tabindex="0" role="note">
        
        
        <p style="margin:1.0em 0.0px;line-height:normal"><span style="font-size:12.0px"><span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif"><b><u><span><font color="#000000">B/E Aerospace </font></span></u></b></span></span><br>
<span style="font-size:12.0px"><span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif">B/E Aerospace, a wholly owned subsidiary of Rockwell Collins Inc., is a leading manufacturer of aircraft interior products and solutions.</span></span><br>
</p>

<p style="margin:1.0em 0.0px;line-height:normal"><span style="font-size:12.0px"><span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif">The Executive Aircraft Seating division manufactures interior products for business jets. Realize your full potential, in our dynamic and fast-paced environment where ideas, talents and experiences are valued. It is conveniently located between Miami and Ft. Lauderdale, Florida.</span></span><br>
</p>

<p style="margin:1.0em 0.0px;line-height:normal"><span style="font-size:12.0px"><span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif">As a leader in the aerospace industry, we are growing rapidly and have a number of exciting positions available right now, including a <strong>Mechanical Design Engineer </strong>in our <strong>Executive Aircraft Seating </strong>business located in <strong>Medley, FL.</strong></span></span><br>
</p>

<p><span style="font-size:12.0px"><span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif"><strong><u>JOB SUMMARY</u></strong></span></span></p>

<p><span style="font-size:12.0px"><span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif">Reporting to the<strong>Engineering Manager,</strong> the <strong>Mechanical Design Engineer </strong>will be responsible to do the planning and design of mechanical equipment; and the oversight of the installation, operation and maintenance of the equipment. </span></span><span style="font-size:12.0px"><span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif">In addition, responsibilities include performing standard engineering assignments usually representing a significant portion of a larger project as well as selecting engineering techniques to solve problems and make design recommendations.</span></span></p>

<p></p>

<p><span style="font-size:12.0px"><span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif"><strong><u>JOB RESPONSIBILITIES</u></strong></span></span></p>

<p><span style="font-size:12.0px"><span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif">Essential duties and responsibilities include the following:</span></span></p>

<p></p>

<ul>
	<li><span style="font-size:12.0px"><span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif">Participates as a team member in a specific phase of a broad engineering assignment.</span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:12.0px"><span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif">Directs preparation of appropriate documentation for assigned projects.</span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:12.0px"><span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif">Provides technical leadership to a small group of temporarily assigned engineers and technicians.</span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:12.0px"><span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif">Ensures successful completion of the assigned project phase within the budgeted time and cost constraints.</span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:12.0px"><span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif">Participates in defining engineering approaches, and in planning and scheduling work.</span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:12.0px"><span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif">Performs other related duties as required.</span></span></li>
</ul>

<p></p>

<p><span style="font-size:12.0px"><span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif"><strong><u>QUALIFICATIONS </u></strong></span></span></p>

<p><span style="font-size:12.0px"><span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif">To perform this job successfully, an individual must be able to perform each essential duty satisfactorily. The requirements listed below are representative of the knowledge, skill, and/or ability required. Reasonable accommodations may be made to enable individuals with disabilities to perform the essential functions.</span></span></p>

<p></p>

<p><span style="font-size:12.0px"><span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif"><strong><u>EDUCATION and/or EXPERIENCE </u></strong></span></span></p>

<ul>
	<li><span style="font-size:12.0px"><span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif">Bachelor's degree in Engineering from four-year college or university.</span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:12.0px"><span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif">A minimum of three years related experience and/or training.</span></span></li>
</ul>

<p></p>

<p><span style="font-size:12.0px"><span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif"><strong><u>LANGUAGE SKILLS </u></strong></span></span></p>

<ul>
	<li><span style="font-size:12.0px"><span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif">Ability to read, analyze, and interpret general business periodicals, professional journals, technical procedures, or governmental regulations.</span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:12.0px"><span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif">Ability to write reports, business correspondence, and procedure manuals.</span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:12.0px"><span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif">Ability to effectively present information and respond to questions from groups of managers, associates, clients, customers, and the general public.</span></span></li>
</ul>

<p></p>

<p><span style="font-size:12.0px"><span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif"><strong><u>MATHEMATICAL SKILLS </u></strong></span></span></p>

<ul>
	<li><span style="font-size:12.0px"><span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif">Ability to apply advanced mathematical concepts such as exponents, logarithms, quadratic equations, and permutations.</span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:12.0px"><span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif">Ability to apply mathematical operations to such tasks as frequency distribution, determination of test reliability and validity, analysis of variance, correlation techniques, sampling theory, and factor analysis.</span></span></li>
</ul>

<p></p>

<p><span style="font-size:12.0px"><span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif"><strong><u>REASONING ABILITY </u></strong></span></span></p>

<ul>
	<li><span style="font-size:12.0px"><span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif">Ability to solve practical problems and deal with a variety of concrete variables in situations where only limited standardization exists.</span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:12.0px"><span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif">Ability to interpret a variety of instructions furnished in written, oral, diagram, or schedule form.</span></span></li>
</ul>

<p></p>

<p><span style="font-size:12.0px"><span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif"><strong><u>PHYSICAL DEMANDS </u></strong></span></span></p>

<p><span style="font-size:12.0px"><span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif">The physical demands described here are representative of those that must be met by an associate to successfully perform the essential functions of this job. Reasonable accommodations may be made to enable individuals with disabilities to perform the essential functions.</span></span></p>

<p></p>

<p><span style="font-size:12.0px"><span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif">While performing the duties of this job, the associate is regularly required to sit; use hands to finger, handle, or feel; talk or hear; and occasionally required to stand; walk; reach with hands and arms; climb or balance; stoop, kneel, crouch, or crawl. The associate must occasionally lift and/or move up to 10 pounds.</span></span></p>

<p></p>

<p><span style="font-size:12.0px"><span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif">Specific vision abilities required by this job include close vision, distance vision, color vision, peripheral vision, depth perception, and ability to adjust focus.</span></span></p>

<p></p>

<p><span style="font-size:12.0px"><span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif"><strong><u>WORK ENVIRONMENT </u></strong></span></span></p>

<p><span style="font-size:12.0px"><span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif">The work environment characteristics described here are representative of those an associate encounters while performing the essential functions of this job. Reasonable accommodations may be made to enable individuals with disabilities to perform the essential functions.</span></span></p>

<p></p>

<p><span style="font-size:12.0px"><span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif">The noise level in the work environment is usually quiet.</span></span></p>

<p></p>

<p><span style="font-size:12.0px"><span style="font-family:Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif"><font color="#000000">The above description reflects the details considered necessary to describe the principal functions of the job and should not be construed as a detailed descriptions of all the work requirements that may be performed in the job. </font></span></span></p>
        <p>EOE/Minorities/Females/Veterans/Disabled. All qualified applicants will receive consideration for employment without regard to race, color, religion, sex, sexual orientation, gender identity, national origin, disability or protected veteran status.</p>

<script type="text/javascript"><!--

var emailDailogBox = null;
var captcha = null;
var emailJobReqId = null;
var emailSourceButton = null;
var jobReqEmailLocale;
var sendButton = null;
var isCaptchaDisable = gebi('isCaptchaDisable').value;
var isOldCaptchaEnabled = gebi('isOldCaptchaEnabled').value;
var refocusElementId = null;

function emailJobReq(jobReqId, sourceButton, title, emailLocale, refocusId) {
  emailJobReqId = jobReqId;
  emailSourceButton = sourceButton;
  jobReqEmailLocale = emailLocale;
  refocusElementId = refocusId;

  //gebi('jobtitlediv').innerHTML = title;
  juic.$('jobtitlediv').innerHTML = '<div tabindex="0"><span class="hiddenAriaContent">Job title:</span>' + title + '</div>';

  if (emailDailogBox == null) {
  var height = '510px';
    if(isCaptchaDisable == true || isCaptchaDisable == 'true'){
	    height = '400px';
    }
    emailDailogBox = new BasicDialog('emailBox', '522px', height, true, {focusId:"emailTitleText", xbutton:"closeAbout", enterkey:true, useIconFonts:true});
  }
  emailDailogBox.show(sourceButton);
  
  gebi(emailBox.id).style.overflow = 'visible';

	
  var xbutton = SFDom.getElementsByClassName("container-close");
  if(xbutton[0]){
     xbutton[0].setAttribute("id","xbuttonId");
     xbutton[0].setAttribute("tabindex","0");
	 //xbutton[0].setAttribute("onblur","setFocus(event);");
	 xbutton[0].setAttribute('title','Close Button');
  
  		// adding event listener
  		 SFDOMEvent.addListener(xbutton[0], "keypress", function closeButtonHandler(e) {
           if (e.keyCode === 13 || e.keyCode === 0 || e.keyCode === 32) {
			    SFDOMEvent.preventDefault(e);
	    	   	emailDailogBox.hide(emailSourceButton);
				if(refocusElementId) {
					SFDom.setFocus(refocusElementId);
				//	SFDOMEvent.removeListener(xbutton[0],'keypress',xyz);
				}
            }
         }, false);
       }

  // clear error message string
  gebi('emailerrorstr').innerHTML = '';

  hide('emailerrors');
  hide('emailsuccess');

  gebi('mailjob_message').value='I saw this job and thought you might be interested in this opportunity.';

  if (sendButton) {
    sendButton.disabled = false;
    Element.addClassName(sendButton.parentNode.parentNode, 'active');
    gebi('closeAbout').innerHTML = 'Cancel';
  }
	if(isCaptchaDisable == 'false' || isCaptchaDisable == false){
     if (isOldCaptchaEnabled == 'false' || isOldCaptchaEnabled == false) {
	  if(!captcha ){
			setTimeout(function(){
				document.getElementById('captchaImg').innerHTML = SFreCAPTCHA.renderCaptchaImage();
				SFreCAPTCHA.setRequired(true);
				document.getElementById('captchaText').innerHTML = SFreCAPTCHA.renderCaptchaText();
				SFreCAPTCHA.create("6LcCg8wSAAAAANPY_SYuAMe7l_dObfxYaukMvFhy","en");
			},500);
			captcha=true;
		} else {
			setTimeout(function(){
			SFreCAPTCHA.reload();},500);
		}
	}
	if (isOldCaptchaEnabled == 'true' || isOldCaptchaEnabled == true) {
		getNewCaptcha();
	}
	}
}


function sendHandler(_sendButton) {
  sendButton = _sendButton
  sendButton.disabled = true;
  Element.removeClassName(sendButton.parentNode.parentNode, 'active');

  var params = [];

  // here build JSON object with 7 parameters and send it to cjsup
  params.push('?m=FBEMailJobReq');
  params.push('&', 'company', '=', 'BEAerospace');
  params.push('&', 'site', '=', 
    encodeURIComponent(gebi('site').value));
  params.push('&', 'rcm_site_locale', '=', 'en_US');
  params.push('&', 'mailjob_job_req_id', '=', emailJobReqId);
  params.push('&', 'mailjob_friend_email', '=', encodeURIComponent(gebi('mailjob_friend_email').value));
  params.push('&', 'mailjob_email_locale','=', jobReqEmailLocale);
  if(isCaptchaDisable == 'false' || isCaptchaDisable == false){
  if (isOldCaptchaEnabled == 'true' || isOldCaptchaEnabled == true) {
      params.push('&', 'mailjob_captcha_value', '=', encodeURIComponent(gebi('mailjob_captcha_value').value));
      params.push('&', 'mailjob_user_captcha_value', '=', encodeURIComponent(gebi('mailjob_user_captcha_value').value));
  } else {
	  params.push('&', 'recaptcha_challenge_field', '=', encodeURIComponent(gebi('recaptcha_challenge_field').value));
	  params.push('&', 'recaptcha_response_field', '=', encodeURIComponent(gebi('recaptcha_response_field').value));
  }
  }
  params.push('&', 'mailjob_user_email', '=', encodeURIComponent(gebi('mailjob_user_email').value));
  params.push('&', 'mailjob_message', '=', encodeURIComponent(gebi('mailjob_message').value));
  params.push('&', 'mailjob_is_public_intranet', '=', 'false');
  params.push('&', '_s.crb', '=', 'nHhXCxNyZUzFL2giqcLKVVd0k9E%3d');

  // recruiting.js should be included by now..
  var url = "/rcmcjsup" + params.join("");

  var errorFree = true;

  if (url.length > 2048) {
    errorFree = false;
    var params_length = [];
    
    // here build JSON object with 4 parameters, including a parameter specifying the url exceedance and send it to cjsup
    params_length.push('?m=FBEMailJobReq');
    params_length.push('&', 'company', '=', 'BEAerospace');
    params_length.push('&', 'rcm_site_locale', '=', 'en_US');
    params_length.push('&', 'mailjob_job_req_id', '=', emailJobReqId);
    params_length.push('&', '_s.crb', '=', 'nHhXCxNyZUzFL2giqcLKVVd0k9E%3d');
    params_length.push('&', 'mailjob_beyond_length', '=', encodeURIComponent(url.length - 2048));
    url = "/rcmcjsup" + params_length.join("");
    
    // Send ajax query to get a message of how much characters need to be removed.
    submitExternalAjaxQuery(url);
    gebi('emailerrorstr').innerHTML = items[0];
    show('emailerrors');
    hide('emailsuccess');
	gebi('emailerrorstr').focus();
  }

  if (errorFree && submitExternalAjaxQuery(url)) {
    if ("undefined" != typeof items) {
      for (var i = 0; i < items.length; i++) {
        if (errorFree) {
          gebi('emailerrorstr').innerHTML = '';
          show('emailerrors');
        }
        errorFree = false;
        gebi('emailerrorstr').innerHTML += (i == 0 ? '' : '<br>') + items[i]['error'];
        hide('emailsuccess');
		gebi('emailerrorstr').focus();
      }
	  if(isCaptchaDisable == 'false' || isCaptchaDisable == false){
      if(!errorFree && (isOldCaptchaEnabled == 'true' || isOldCaptchaEnabled == true)) {
    	  getNewCaptcha();
    	  gebi('mailjob_user_captcha_value').value = '';
      }
	}
    }
  }

  if (errorFree) {
    gebi('closeAbout').innerHTML = 'Close';
    //gebi('closeAbout').focus();
    show('emailsuccess');
    var emailId = '';
    if(req && req.responseText) {
      var responseObject = JSON.parse(req.responseText);
      if ("undefined" != typeof responseObject) {
        emailId = responseObject.friendEmail;
      }
    }
    gebi('confirmmessage').innerHTML = 'The job has been sent to' + ' '
        + emailId + '.';
    hide('emailerrors');
	gebi('mailjob_friend_email').value = '';
    gebi('mailjob_message').value='I saw this job and thought you might be interested in this opportunity.';
	if(isCaptchaDisable == 'false' || isCaptchaDisable == false){
    if (isOldCaptchaEnabled == 'true' || isOldCaptchaEnabled == true) {
        gebi('mailjob_user_captcha_value').value = '';
    	getNewCaptcha();
    }
  if (isOldCaptchaEnabled == 'false' || isOldCaptchaEnabled == false) {
	gebi('recaptcha_response_field').value = '';
	SFreCAPTCHA.reload();
  }
  }
  gebi('emailsuccess').focus();
  }
  sendButton.disabled = false;
  Element.addClassName(sendButton.parentNode.parentNode, 'active');
}

function getNewCaptcha() {
  if (submitExternalAjaxQuery("/rcmcjsup?m=createCaptchaString&company=BEAerospace&tstamp=" + (new Date()).getTime())) {
    if ("undefined" != typeof items) {
      gebi('mailjob_captcha_value').value = items;
      var refreshImgURL = "/imgsource?imgStr=" + items + "&_s.crb=" + ajaxSecKey;
      gebi('captcha_image').src = refreshImgURL;
    }
  }
}

function reFocus(){
if(gebi(refocusElementId)){
   document.getElementById(refocusElementId).focus();
   }
}

        }
        
        //Save to jobcart
        function saveToJobCart()
	    {
		    var strTemp;
		    var lIdx;
		    var lLen;
		    var arrSubInfo;

		    if (document.frmJobDetail.jobcartcnt.value > 50)
			    alert (MSG_cim_jobdetail_JobCart);
		    else
		    {
			    document.frmSaveToCart.chkJobClientIds.value = ReplaceInString(document.frmSaveToCart.chkJobClientIds.value, "%%", "");
			    arrSubInfo = document.frmSaveToCart.chkJobClientIds.value.split("|");		    

			    if(arrSubInfo.length != 3)
			    {
				    strTemp =  arrSubInfo[0] + "|" + arrSubInfo[1];
				    document.frmSaveToCart.chkJobClientIds.value = strTemp;
			    }
			    openWindow3('about:blank?sessionid=7b19d835f79eba455f9b26dac02334327b7d');
			    document.frmSaveToCart.submit();
		    }
	    }

	    function reload(sParam)
	    {
		if (typeof(sParam) != 'undefined') 
		{
			if (sParam == 'ApplyAsRegularJob')
				ApplyAsRegularJob();
			return;
		}
		var sGQId =  "0";
		var arrGQId;
		var iLen = 0;
		if (sGQId == '' )
		{
			sGQId= document.frmJobDetail.JobInfo.value;
			arrGQId = (sGQId.substring(2, sGQId.length - 2)).split("%%");
			iLen = arrGQId.length;
		}
		
		if ((iLen == 1) || (sGQId != ''))
		{
			 
		document.frmJobDetail.target = "_self";
		 
		document.frmJobDetail.action = "Logout.aspx?SID=^I9ikivcLCmNq7dY0llL7KBgncM01olc053PCnv52Jkh7qwj3CCzoTSWdO8zKZ_slp_rhc_/A&gqclose=yes&crl=yes&Exit=^VPbBpv82eWbDhCwKzWDUrT6iCUhsWNOr+koga53E/lzXlNjlAug5wQQ9zAIHEB3h/wTIH+ld1Juf/KBSJ9E2P2Se9/ttvXnZ6Bu9ZP6AGTfBQR7IwInWtPQYijGsqumBUnZPYe/JaIxy3Geqq8xGSn6eHPQ8CrSOtrh5gO9VSRsNUxRXry6MnrQ8ZStMY2dOOaw7yqMZcTkyEugM2NTZxfGFiXU1RJgFdWwafkpt06yDdh8vDsG3L6rUhdfSMTjohr7+iZr8H041gl6lo2KLs4RMGaWN0K2zvKJphjmVUvLlRRzHqdPu5V8wc4JSith+0l8yizbJhTeB8rle9gtQBVkjoyvFB9RXT3bImw/ukzcTkC4iao1HKQ==";

class='Fieldlabel'> <label id='lblWhyCDMSmith?'>Why CDM Smith?</label> </span></td><td width='80%' class='TGAlignLeft'> <span class='TEXT' id='Why CDM Smith?' aria-labelledby='lblWhyCDMSmith?' >CDM Smith is a major partner to the Federal Emergency Management Agency (FEMA), supporting its mission under various prime and/or sub-prime contracts for Public Assistance, Individual Assistance, Hazard Mitigation Assistance, and Risk Analysis. The Public Assistance program supports recovery operations primarily for debris removal, emergency protective measures, and the repair, replacement, or restoration of disaster-damaged, publicly-owned facilities, such as: roads, bridges, municipal buildings, police and fire stations, water/wastewater treatment plants, etc., including Private Non-Profit facilities such as hospitals. The Hazard Mitigation assistance program supports operations to reduce the risk to life and property; including the existing build environment and future construction, in the pre and post disaster environments through regulations, local ordinances, land use and building practices.</span> </td></tr><tr> <td valign='top'><span class='Fieldlabel'> <label id='lblJobDescription'>Job Description</label> </span></td><td width='80%' class='TGAlignLeft'> <span class='TEXT' id='Job Description' aria-labelledby='lblJobDescription' >We are currently accepting resumes for future project work. Qualified candidates will be contacted once next steps have been identified.<br/><br/>General Responsibilities May Include:<br/> Conducting preliminary damage assessments (PDAs) in the field with Federal, State and local officials.<br/> Writing Project Worksheets (PWs) for the purposes of determining project eligibility, scopes of work and estimating costs to repair or replace a facility or structure in order to restore it to its pre-disaster design.<br/> Providing technical, cost estimating, disaster recovery and/or management services with an emphasis on engineering and the understanding of design principles and engineering specifications.<br/> Offering solutions to engineering problems.</span> </td></tr><tr> <td valign='top'><span class='Fieldlabel'> <label id='lblMinimumQualifications'>Minimum Qualifications</label> </span></td><td width='80%' class='TGAlignLeft'> <span class='TEXT' id='Minimum Qualifications' aria-labelledby='lblMinimumQualifications' > A Bachelors Degree in Engineering is required; professional designation such as PE is preferred.<br/> A minimum of 2 years of relevant experience is required.<br/> Preference will be given to candidates with one or more of the following FEMA Public Assistance classroom trainings: Public Assistance Operations I (PA Ops I), Public Assistance Operations II (PA Ops II), Project Worksheet (PW) Development, Cost Estimating Format (CEF), Debris Management/Operations, 406 Hazard Mitigation. <br/> Prior FEMA Public Assistance disaster response and recovery experience in one of the following areas: Public Assistance Coordinator (PAC) Crew Leader, Project Specialist, Debris Specialist, Debris Monitor, FEMA-certified Trainer, Hazard Mitigation Specialist (Sections 404 and 406), or Long Term Community Recovery Program Specialist is strongly desired.<br/> Must be a U.S. citizen and be able to pass an FBI background check.<br/> Ability to mobilize within 24-48 hours, commit to a minimum 90-day assignment in remote locations and disaster conditions. <br/> Due to the nature of the work, candidates must have excellent communication skills and be experienced with Microsoft Office product suite.</span> </td></tr><tr> <td valign='top'><span class='Fieldlabel'> <label id='lblAssignmentCategory'>Assignment Category</label> </span></td><td width='80%' class='TGAlignLeft'> <span
